    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer13965115281836765180"><b>No one wants to be single at the holidays.</b> <br/> <br/>Even Little Miss Grinch, Nikki, a successful and independent woman, must face her bachelorette status at the most horrible time of the year. <br/> <br/>December is her personal version of holly-jolly hell: a merry torture made of couples kissing at every corner, forced vacation days, and an inescapable family reunion. <br/> <br/>And when her baby si</span>
  <span id="freeText13965115281836765180" style="display:none"><b>No one wants to be single at the holidays.</b> <br /> <br />Even Little Miss Grinch, Nikki, a successful and independent woman, must face her bachelorette status at the most horrible time of the year. <br /> <br />December is her personal version of holly-jolly hell: a merry torture made of couples kissing at every corner, forced vacation days, and an inescapable family reunion. <br /> <br />And when her baby sister announces she’s engaged—to Paul, the man Nikki is secretly in love with—and that he’s spending the holidays with them, Christmas starts looking bluer than ever. <br /> <br />Nikki can’t possibly survive an entire week trapped home as the family’s spinster. But she has no time to meet men or to try the newest dating app, she’s too busy working as a video producer for an advertising agency. <br /> <br />So what’s a girl to do? <br /> <br />Nikki has the perfect solution:<b> to hire a fake boyfriend.</b> <br /> <br />Luckily, her job gives her access to an endless catalog of gorgeous actors to choose from. <br /> <br />But Nikki will soon discover that keeping business and pleasure from mixing isn’t so easy, and that she might not be immune to a little mistletoe magic. Especially not when she picked out the perfect man as her Christmas date... <br /> <br />A fun, festive romantic comedy with lots of bad behavior and Christmas spirit. Like a creamy hot chocolate with marshmallows, you won’t want to put this deliciously hilarious novel down. Perfect for fans of Sophie Kinsella, Sally Thorne, and Jo Watson. <br /> <br />First Comes Love is a series of interconnected romantic novels. However, each book in the series can be read as a standalone. <br /></span>

      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_sort_order_span_tip_452').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38946743-berit?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38946743-berit?shelf=blog-tour">blog-tour</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2575436918" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14323692470683766817">I absolutely adored and loved every single word in this book!<br/><br/>If you could see me you would see that I have a BIG smile on my face, I have found me another wonderful author! I love a book that completely engages you and captures your heart! The storyline in this book was not original, in fact it has been done many times before and the author even mentions that in the book... but these characters were so electric, they completely drew me in!<br/><br/>Nikki is not in the holiday mood, in fact she wouldn’t mi</span>
  <span id="freeText14323692470683766817" style="display:none">I absolutely adored and loved every single word in this book!<br /><br />If you could see me you would see that I have a BIG smile on my face, I have found me another wonderful author! I love a book that completely engages you and captures your heart! The storyline in this book was not original, in fact it has been done many times before and the author even mentions that in the book... but these characters were so electric, they completely drew me in!<br /><br />Nikki is not in the holiday mood, in fact she wouldn’t mind skipping the entire month of December... when she finds out her sister is bringing her new fiancé to Christmas she goes into full Scrooge mode... The worst part her sister’s fiancé Paul, a man she’s had a crush on since college.... determined not to go home for Christmas single and with no time to find a date Nikki decides to hire a date.... as I said this is a popular trope that has been done before, but I have to admit it is one of my favorites!<br /><br />Nikki is a fantastic character I loved her, I mean what’s not to love the girl is a cat lover! She is also smart and sassy.... I adored her relationship with her BFF Blair... but most of all I loved the banter and chemistry between Nicky and hired date Diego.... Diego was such a good guy, down-to-earth and genuine, the kind of guy you would want to take home to your parents... not to mention he was tall, dark, and handsome... The perfect go to parade in front of your sister, I make her a little bit jealous.... add in some family drama, Christmas festivities, gluten-free food, adorable animals, and you have got yourself one wonderful story!<br /><br />Absolutely recommend, this is one of the best Christmas romances I have Red this season!<br /><br />*** A huge thank you to the author and Rachelle for my copy of this book ***</span>

  <span id="freeText4799794135706481241" style="display:none">Oh how I LOVED this book! This is my first Camilla Isley book and I can’t wait to read all her others! I have been searching high and low for the perfect romcom and I’ve finally found it. Best Christmas book of the season!<br /><br />Nikki is a successful, single career woman who is reluctantly going home for the holidays. After finally deciding that she’s had enough with her family questioning why she’s still single, she decides to take matters into her own hands.<br /><br />I loved these characters and their antics and the oh so perfect and smoldering love interest. I mean, a beautiful man who is nice AND cleans up after himself? That’s a keeper!<br /><br />This also has the perfect amount of Christmas atmosphere – from snowman building to holiday meal prep – you will find yourself catching the holiday spirit while reading.<br />There is something to be said about a book that can make you laugh out loud and you will find that here. If you’re like me and read for entertainment, you will most definitely find yourself entertained!<br /><br />Thank you again to Rachel and Camilla. This book is now available!</span>

  <span id="freeText16593462387519957192" style="display:none"><b>4 super cute and funny stars to A Christmas Date!</b> 🎄 🎄 🎄 🎄 <br /><br />After not being much of a holiday book reader in my reading life, this year, I’ve been on a spree of collecting holiday reads. A Christmas Date is a standout amongst the pack. <br /><br />Nikki is not a fan of the holidays. Being single and independently so is hard this time of year. When she would rather be working, she is forced to take time off and observe how romantic everyone feels about Christmas. <br /><br />Everything comes to a head wine Nikki’s sister announces her engagement to a man Nikki has feelings for (but no one knows). Not only that, but he is spending the holidays with the family in celebration. <br /><br />Nikki needs to survive this week at home and look good doing it, so she hires a fake boyfriend. She quickly finds a handsome actor to play the part. However, what will happen if Nikki finds the magical romance of the holidays charming her, too? <br /><br />A Christmas Date is an endearingly funny romantic comedy perfect for an holiday pick-me-up. It’s soothing, comforting, and super cute. I read it in one quick sitting. Thanks to my friends, Melisa and Berit for the recommendation.<br /><br />Thanks also to the publisher for the complimentary copy. All opinions are my own. <br /><br />My reviews can also be found on my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jennifertarheelreader.com">www.jennifertarheelreader.com</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2576738425?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whispering Stories" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whispering Stories" href="/user/show/20354973-whispering-stories">Whispering Stories</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2576738425" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7392623839833603086">Book Reviewed by Stacey on <a href='https://www.whisperingstories.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>www.whisperingstories.com</a><br/><br/>Nikki has been in love with Paul for many years since they were teenagers but when Paul started dating her younger sister Julia a couple of years ago she knew he was out of bounds forever and it broke her heart.<br/><br/>When her sister announces, just before Christmas, that the two are engaged Nikki puts on a brave face but is absolutely devastated. Then she learns that when she goes home to her parents for Christmas the loved-up Julia and Paul will be </span>
  <span id="freeText7392623839833603086" style="display:none">Book Reviewed by Stacey on <a href="https://www.whisperingstories.com" rel="nofollow noopener">www.whisperingstories.com</a><br /><br />Nikki has been in love with Paul for many years since they were teenagers but when Paul started dating her younger sister Julia a couple of years ago she knew he was out of bounds forever and it broke her heart.<br /><br />When her sister announces, just before Christmas, that the two are engaged Nikki puts on a brave face but is absolutely devastated. Then she learns that when she goes home to her parents for Christmas the loved-up Julia and Paul will be staying too, upset about being around the pair for a week she takes drastic action.<br /><br />Nikki hires male model Diego, to be her ‘boyfriend’ for the holidays and with Diego being Julia’s ideal man, Nikki is even more impressed with her choice as she can’t wait for her sister to be so jealous of her. But will her plan work?<br /><br />I love Camilla Isley’s books as they bring together lots of humour, great characters and romantic moments that are always bursting at the seams. A Christmas Date is no exception.<br /><br />From opening the first page to the very last, I was addicted. The bickering sisters, parents who are at the ends of their wits with their daughters, a handsome fake date and the best, best friend a girl could ask for, plus a dog that thinks he’s a cat!! What’s not to like?<br /><br />This book is pure enjoyment the whole way through. The plot was a little predictable at times, but this didn’t lessen my enjoyment as Camilla’s writing style is so engaging and exciting.<br /><br />This is the third book in a series, though it can be read as a stand-alone too. It wasn’t until I was partway through that I realised that I had read book two in the series as well – Doh.<br /><br />If you love rom-coms this is the book to read, especially at this time of year with it being set over Christmas. It is just delightful. It is also heart-warming too and will put a smile on your face.</span>

The characters were competitive, stressed to a toxic level, and nearing the obnoxious register on the pettiness scale with life-long sibling rivalries reaching a scalding level. But what family holiday gathering isn’t complete without several meltdowns and a messy food skirmish? It’s not even Halloween yet and I’m already in the Christmas spirit and dreaming of the heavily laden table – bring on the pie.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2659586266253730456">4☆ A Cosy Festive Romance.<br/><br/>First of all I want to start by saying how festive the cover is I love it, it sums up A Christmas Date.<br/><br/>A Christmas Date is the third book in the series, but my first book. I had absolutely no problem quickly settling into the story. <br/><br/>I really enjoyed reading this Warm, Cosy, feel good, light hearted Romp. <br/>It had Romance, Fun, Family Drama, sibling rivalry, Mishaps, Sass, Fake Dates, Secrets, all around the Festive Season.<br/><br/>Nikki hates Christmas, but most of all she hates s</span>
  <span id="freeText2659586266253730456" style="display:none">4☆ A Cosy Festive Romance.<br /><br />First of all I want to start by saying how festive the cover is I love it, it sums up A Christmas Date.<br /><br />A Christmas Date is the third book in the series, but my first book. I had absolutely no problem quickly settling into the story. <br /><br />I really enjoyed reading this Warm, Cosy, feel good, light hearted Romp. <br />It had Romance, Fun, Family Drama, sibling rivalry, Mishaps, Sass, Fake Dates, Secrets, all around the Festive Season.<br /><br />Nikki hates Christmas, but most of all she hates spending it with her judgemental family.<br />You see Nikki's sister Jules is perfect in every way and now she is about to blow Nikki's world apart!<br /><br />Jules has just announced shes engaged to boyfriend Paul.<br />Why would that bother Nikki???...... well Nikki is head over heels... hopelessly in Love with Paul! They knew each other from way back But Nikki missed her chance.<br /><br />After hearing the news about the engagement, Nikki decides the only way she is going to get through the holidays is to hire herself a Fake Boyfriend.<br />So she enters a few details into her Advertising works database and.... finds Diego!<br />Five thousand dollars later, a promise of an Audition for the Super Bowl Commercial and Diego is hired!<br /><br />Diego is Tall, Dark, Handsome and Smouldering HOT!!.... everything that Nikki's sister Jules finds sexually attractive.<br /><br />But in order for them to make their Fake Relationship work, Nikki decides to move Diego into her flat temporarily so they can become acquainted with each other.<br /><br />Ok so..... Nikki has hired Diego to make Jules jealous, shut her family up, and make going home for Christmas that lil bit more bearable.<br />I mean what could possibly go wrong?!?!<br /><br />Camilla has created a captivating, witty and fun Romantic Romp.<br />The characters are likeable, endearing, real, and Nikki and Diego quickly became my favourite characters. I loved their cheeky flirty banter between them.<br />The pace just flows along, I simply devoured it in two nights.<br /><br />I highly recommend this adorable book if you are wanting a festive feel good read, that will sweep you away with Romance, Drama and Cheeky Banter the perfect Rom Com / Chick Lit.<br />So grab a hot chocolate and snuggle down.<br /><br />Thank you to Rachel Random Resources for this copy which I reviewed honestly and voluntarily.<br /><br />My Review is also on my Blog Website :-<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://dashfan81.blogspot.com/2018/11/blog-tour-christmas-date.html">https://dashfan81.blogspot.com/2018/1...</a></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer993570816392552039">So so good! I’m feeling the Christmas spirit in November and this is not like me. Camilla Isley won me over and I’m totally in love with my new book boyfriend Diego (Mr Perfect). <br/><br/>I’m a fan of fake relationships and this one is perfectly executed. Nikki is very successful in her career. She is not very lucky when it comes to love. In fact, her sister is dating the man of her dreams and Nikki just wants to get through the holidays unscathed. In the run-up to Christmas Nikki tries to avoid long con</span>
  <span id="freeText993570816392552039" style="display:none">So so good! I’m feeling the Christmas spirit in November and this is not like me. Camilla Isley won me over and I’m totally in love with my new book boyfriend Diego (Mr Perfect). <br /><br />I’m a fan of fake relationships and this one is perfectly executed. Nikki is very successful in her career. She is not very lucky when it comes to love. In fact, her sister is dating the man of her dreams and Nikki just wants to get through the holidays unscathed. In the run-up to Christmas Nikki tries to avoid long conversations with her family in the hope of not being roped into too many unpleasant memories. Unfortunately this year her sister is about to spring the ultimate unbearable news. Paul is coming home for Christmas with her and they are getting married. Nikki wants to make it through the holidays without all the synthetic family members wondering when she’s going to settle down. After the idea is given to her she decides to get herself a little Christmas present. A man for Christmas. <br /><br />Diego O’Donnell is a struggling actor picked right out of a catalogue. He’s tall, dark and half Italian. He has green smouldering eyes and a badass bike. He’s Nikki’s sister's dream man and perfect for the job. Little does Nikki know he is also sweet, caring and a beautiful person. <br /><br />A Christmas date is fun, festive and loveable. I was hooked on every minute. Yes, it’s cliche and maybe Diego is too perfect for the real world but isn’t that what Christmas is all about? This is the perfect heartwarming Christmas read and I loved it. I will definitely be looking at this authors other books. I think I’ve just become a new fan. Fingers crossed. <br /><br />5 out of 5. It’s great.<br /><br />*I received an ARC in exchange for an honest review via NetGalley.</span>

<div id="review_2578958879" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <span id="freeText12873928908528661853" style="display:none">Beautifully written with wit, humour, romance and festive high jinx. A Christmas Date was a real festive treat that I enjoyed from page one. (The parent guilt trip! – Yep, been there!) To the wonderful ending.<br /><br />I guess that this is a festive trope that will never grow old for me and I love new twists on it. What I go here was a refreshingly funny – I mean really funny- tale. The stressful family Christmas situation, the embarrassment and the arguments that end up being less awful than was expected. This one added so much more Christmas sparkle with the laugh out loud moments and festive warm fuzzies!<br /><br />I am smiling and full of festive spirit<br /><br />Thank you to Rachel’s Random Resources and Camilla Isley for providing me with a review copy of A Christmas Date in exchange for my honest review.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2551609600" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer150870974183759941">If you are thinking what I think, then you guessed it right. This is the textual Christmas version of 'The Wedding Date', but far better than the original book 'Asking for Trouble' of which the movie is based. So we could pretty much see the story through the blurb itself, but that won't deter the reading pleasure a bit. After all, this is a different setting, different girl and if you can visualise someone better looking than Dermot Mulroney, well, then we have a too good to be true hero in our</span>
  <span id="freeText150870974183759941" style="display:none">If you are thinking what I think, then you guessed it right. This is the textual Christmas version of 'The Wedding Date', but far better than the original book 'Asking for Trouble' of which the movie is based. So we could pretty much see the story through the blurb itself, but that won't deter the reading pleasure a bit. After all, this is a different setting, different girl and if you can visualise someone better looking than Dermot Mulroney, well, then we have a too good to be true hero in our hands. <br /> This is the third in the 'First Comes Love' series but can be read as a standalone. Filled with festive spirit, family moments and siblings rivalry, the book makes an unforgettable read which will warm you like a sweet cup of hot chocolate. Nikki and Diego make a charming couple and their love story is as exciting and intriguing as their respective personalities. Within no time, we get attached to both of them and the impact of the fake date arrangement on Jules was priceless. I enjoyed every twist and turn of the plot and the ending was really fitting to a Christmas story. Highly recommended !!!</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irena BookDustMagic" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irena BookDustMagic" href="/user/show/17737927-irena-bookdustmagic">Irena BookDustMagic</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2578971100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3703508778424383808">First of all, I think this book has the longest synopsis ever, so I won’t repeat what it is about, just read them if you’re interested (or don’t if you’re like me, and like to go into books blind).<br/><br/>Camilla Isley is the author who’s books I noticed before and some of them are on my tbr list, but I still didn’t read them for one reason or another (you know how it goes, too many books, so little time and similar excuses).<br/>When I saw her email in my mailbox I was surprised, to say the least. I always </span>
  <span id="freeText3703508778424383808" style="display:none">First of all, I think this book has the longest synopsis ever, so I won’t repeat what it is about, just read them if you’re interested (or don’t if you’re like me, and like to go into books blind).<br /><br />Camilla Isley is the author who’s books I noticed before and some of them are on my tbr list, but I still didn’t read them for one reason or another (you know how it goes, too many books, so little time and similar excuses).<br />When I saw her email in my mailbox I was surprised, to say the least. I always admired her from away, and to see that she knows who I am and wants me to review her book was a pleasant shock.<br /><br />I had so much fun reading A Christmas Date. It was quick and quirky, and it made me laugh out loud. <br />I liked the story. It does have some cliches, but I didn’t mind them.<br /><br />What I liked the most was the writing style. Reading this novel was easy as drinking, I just flew through it, and before I realized, the story was over.<br />It was short and sweet, just like a chick-lit novels should be.<br /><br />I mean, A Christmas Date is a chick lit at it’s best.<br /><br />What I also liked about this book is how it explores siblings relationship, including rivalry and affection.<br /><br />I liked almost all the characters from the book. The only one I wasn’t a fan of was Nikki’s sister, but then again, since Nikki has love/hate relationship with her, and the story is written from Nikki’s POV, I think Julia was ment to be unlikeable.<br /><br />This is a festive read, but since Nikki has somewhat Grinchy approach to holidays, it was refreshing to read about Christmas in a different light.<br />However, even Nikki’s grumpy attitude couldn’t kill the Christmas spirit of the story.<br /><br />Overall, I really enjoyed reading A Christmas Date and am looking forward to read Isley’s other books.<br /><br />I would recommend this book to everyone who is in the mood for some merry chick lit.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3703508778424383808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kati " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kati " href="/user/show/6553210-kati">Kati </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2610310100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8951930107162856319">*** I received this book through NetGalley in exchange for an honest review, thank you so much to NetGalley and Pink Bloom Press for the opportunity to read and review A Christmas Date! ***<br/><br/>I would like to sincerely apologize to Pink Bloom Press for posted a late review for A Christmas Date now just 2018 was not a great year for me health-wise and I am still struggling with my health this year as well. But let's go onwards and talk about my review and not talk about my health issues now, shall we</span>
  <span id="freeText8951930107162856319" style="display:none">*** I received this book through NetGalley in exchange for an honest review, thank you so much to NetGalley and Pink Bloom Press for the opportunity to read and review A Christmas Date! ***<br /><br />I would like to sincerely apologize to Pink Bloom Press for posted a late review for A Christmas Date now just 2018 was not a great year for me health-wise and I am still struggling with my health this year as well. But let's go onwards and talk about my review and not talk about my health issues now, shall we? Now back in November, I've been seeing great reviews about this book everywhere in the book blogging community that I was intrigued to check it out my self. Plus it would have been a great Christmas book to read during the festive holiday season, so I went to NetGalley and see if the had it and they did and I was so glad and happy when I got the chance to read it through NetGalley. Ohh I loved and enjoyed this amazing Christmas Romance book mix in with fun and laughter featuring with two headstrong sisters that always biker and fight during there family holiday stay at there parents house always trying to one-up each other. I know there was going to be a complete and utter mess in the family household with hilarity ensue especially when Nikki little sister is engaged to Paul who not only is her best male friend but she secretly was in love with him as well and I was so ready to read messy and hilarious Christmas Romance book. And I am really happy to report that I got everything that I wanted in this book plus more. Now I don't want to go into any details about A Christmas Date because I think you all should read this book and see how you feel about this gem of a book. Now A Christmas Date is the third book of the First Comes Love series and I didn't read the first or second book of the First Comes Love series but I do think you can read this amazing book as a stand-alone. But it did make me want to read the first and second book of First Comes Love series because I loved and enjoyed the writing style that flowed well with understandable fun dialogue. I loved reading all the characters and the family dynamic in A Christmas Date. Yes, the two sisters butt heads all the time and fight to be better than the other but later on, you understand why these two sisters annoy and fights each other and you can truly see they love each other unconditionally at the end of the book. All and all I absolutely and utter loved and enjoyed everything in A Christmas Date that I would like to continue to read more books by Camilla Isley in the future. <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_2555061517" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2555061517" />
    <a title="Rachel Gilbey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5801320-rachel-gilbey"><img alt="Rachel Gilbey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406228319p2/5801320.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2555061517?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Gilbey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Gilbey" href="/user/show/5801320-rachel-gilbey">Rachel Gilbey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2555061517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14899773246966106593">I had been a bit worried going into reading this that I had read something in theory similar sounding only a few months ago, and was worried I wouldn't find this particularly original as a result. <br/><br/>Well I was completely wrong - ok the hiring of a fake date for whatever reason has been done before and the book even makes a point of referencing some films where that is the case in it - so although you are going into this with a fairly good idea of how it may all end up - the journey is still incred</span>
  <span id="freeText14899773246966106593" style="display:none">I had been a bit worried going into reading this that I had read something in theory similar sounding only a few months ago, and was worried I wouldn't find this particularly original as a result. <br /><br />Well I was completely wrong - ok the hiring of a fake date for whatever reason has been done before and the book even makes a point of referencing some films where that is the case in it - so although you are going into this with a fairly good idea of how it may all end up - the journey is still incredibly enjoyable. <br /><br />I absolutely loved this book and found myself whizzing through it. The first thing that amused me about this book is the main character's name - Nikki Moore - as I have read some wonderful books by a real life Nikki Moore. No idea if it was sheer fluke, but I kept thinking of the other one every time the name was written in full! <br /><br />I loved the motivation for Nikki to hire her fake date, and the reasons she had for the criteria of what sort of man she was looking for. I also fell for the man rather fast, he was gorgeous and had a really great vibe to him. <br /><br />The connection between Nikki and Diego was evident the whole time, and there are so many amusing moments in the book . <br /><br />This really is an enjoyable read, and another lovely book from an author that I enjoy more and more each time I read her. <br /><br />Thank you to Camilla Isley for this copy which I have reviewed honestly and voluntarily. </span>

  <span id="freeText15865948413445635853" style="display:none">This book is the third part of a series, but even though I have not read the other ones, I did not have any difficulty in picking up the story.<br /><br />Although Nikki is not really keen on Christmas, this year she might receive more than she bargained for or will it all go up in smoke?<br /><br />I truely enjoyed this book. It's funny, it's playful but it also has a more serious underlayer about rekindling certain relationships and revelations.<br /><br />Winter is slowly creeping up on us as well, so if you want to shut the world out for a few hours, I suggest you snuggle under a blanket, get yourself a hot drink and enjoy this heartwarming and fluently written story.<br /><br />I hope the sequel will be published in the near future. 4 stars.<br /><br />Thank you, Camilla Isley and RachelsRandomResources<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bforbookreview.wordpress.com">https://bforbookreview.wordpress.com</a></span>

<div id="review_2605754308" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2605754308" />
    <a title="Heidi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5463965-heidi"><img alt="Heidi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1326677199p2/5463965.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2605754308?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heidi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heidi" href="/user/show/5463965-heidi">Heidi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2605754308" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12921384617112760187">Four stars: A funny holiday tale with some hilarious developments. <br/><br/>Nikki hates the holiday season, especially since a trip home is looming over her head. She keeps trying to avoid her mother and sister, but then her sister, Julia, shows up wanting to take her to lunch. Things go from bad to the worst when Julia brings Paul, Nikki’s best friend from college, whom she has been crushing on for years. Over lunch, Julia and Paul announce their engagement. The prospect of the holidays just got a whole</span>
  <span id="freeText12921384617112760187" style="display:none">Four stars: A funny holiday tale with some hilarious developments. <br><br>Nikki hates the holiday season, especially since a trip home is looming over her head. She keeps trying to avoid her mother and sister, but then her sister, Julia, shows up wanting to take her to lunch. Things go from bad to the worst when Julia brings Paul, Nikki’s best friend from college, whom she has been crushing on for years. Over lunch, Julia and Paul announce their engagement. The prospect of the holidays just got a whole lot unmerrier as Nikki grapples with the thought of returning home as a spinster and having to watch Julia and Paul together. Desperate, Nikki does something bold and brazen, she hires a boyfriend for the holidays. Diego is smoking hot and he has all the characteristics that Julia longs for in a boyfriend. Will Nikki pull off her fake boyfriend scheme?<br>What I Liked:<br>*The Christmas Date ended up being a delightful holiday read. I admit, it started off a bit rocky as I wasn’t a fan of prickly Nikki, but thankfully I stuck with it and was rewarded. This book is hilarious. It has fun characters, a charming romance and some family brawling. This one made me giggle. <br>*Nikki starts out as a holiday grinch. She has no patience for her mother and sister and she is sick of being single. I wasn’t a big fan of her in the beginning, especially in the way she treated her mom. Thankfully, I warmed up to her character. What I did like about her was her insecurity and her vulnerable side. She is complicated, but as the book goes on I warmed up to her as I saw her grapple with her insecurities. She truly transforms by the end of the book. I loved her at the end. <br>*Diego is the perfect love interest. He is genuine, kind, handsome and he sees through Nikki’s tough exterior to the vulnerable and sweet woman underneath. He handles all the uncomfortable situations with grace and charm. Loved him!<br>*What I loved the most about this one was the complex family dynamics. I thought the author captured the competitive sister relationship perfectly. Julia and Nikki definitely have some sister issues. In fact, they get down right bitchy with one another. No one can needle you like a sibling, and *I loved how the author conveyed the complicated parts of Julia and Nikki’s relationship. The kitchen scene was outstanding. When the food settles, Nikki makes it right because that is what sisters do. Loved this!<br>*The romance is adorable. It starts out under strange circumstances, but over time a friendship is formed before blooming into something more. I loved the heat and chemistry and how things progressed. It was perfect, even with the big stumble. <br>*This book is part of a series, but no worries, it is a companion book and it can be read as a stand alone so jump in. <br>*The ending was sweet and satisfying. It left me with a big, happy grin. This was the best holiday book I read this season. <br>And The Not So Much:<br>*As I mentioned, I was put off by Nikki during the first part of the book. She is jealous, self centered and she doesn’t appreciate her family. Thankfully, over time she gets it and evolves. <br>*This is the type of romance where I kept wanting the male perspective. I so wanted to get into *Diego’s head and see Nikki and her messed up family through his eyes. <br>I wished there was a tiny bit more progression in Nikki’s relationship with her mom. <br><br>The Christmas Date is a hilarious book that chronicles one woman’s desperate attempt to one up her younger sister. This one has romance, family fights, growth, holiday cheer and a food fight. What more do you need for the holidays?<br><br>I received a copy of this book from the publisher in exchange for an honest review. All opinions are my own, and I was not compensated for this review. <br>Posted@<a href="http://www.rainydayramblings.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Rainy Day Ramblings</a>.<br><a href="http://rainydayramblings.typepad.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311755i/688599.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12921384617112760187" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2572999449" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1875060236688382981">I loved everything about this book. Yes, the fake-boyfriend story has been done a million times already but Camilla has a way of taking an old trope and make it fresh and exciting and witty to boot!<br/><br/>The story was hilarious, and Nikki was a wonderful protagonist. I could identify with her so easily, and the best part was that she was able to admit her imperfections (especially to her best friend Blair--they really have the perfect friendship) and still go over the top a little with her crazy solut</span>
  <span id="freeText1875060236688382981" style="display:none">I loved everything about this book. Yes, the fake-boyfriend story has been done a million times already but Camilla has a way of taking an old trope and make it fresh and exciting and witty to boot!<br /><br />The story was hilarious, and Nikki was a wonderful protagonist. I could identify with her so easily, and the best part was that she was able to admit her imperfections (especially to her best friend Blair--they really have the perfect friendship) and still go over the top a little with her crazy solutions.<br /><br />The story has everything from the holidays cheer and mood (notwithstanding Nikki's initial resistance to it), to warm chocolate, Christmas tunes and decoration, family, friendship, an array of super-cute side-kick pets both cats and a cute dog... there are food fights, hilarious sisterly meltdowns, a magical sparkling romance, and a swoon-worthy leading man you'll just want to crown as your next favorite book-boyfriend!<br /><br />A perfect holiday read!<br /><br /><br /></span>

    <a title="ItaPixie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18117041-itapixie"><img alt="ItaPixie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589969103p2/18117041.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13029241122896620542"><p> It was too long since I've read a new chick-lit written by Camilla Isley, this book just refreshed my memory and her fabulous writing style enchanted me once again.<br/><br/>Nikki,our heroine,is a smart and successful businesswoman but she's dreading to go home alone this Christmas because she doesn't want to be pitied by her family so she hires a beautiful guy to be her fake boyfriend for the week,easy peasy,right?But she didn't remember that Christmas is a magic time and sometimes also the unthinkable </p></span>
  <span id="freeText13029241122896620542" style="display:none"><p> It was too long since I've read a new chick-lit written by Camilla Isley, this book just refreshed my memory and her fabulous writing style enchanted me once again.<br /><br />Nikki,our heroine,is a smart and successful businesswoman but she's dreading to go home alone this Christmas because she doesn't want to be pitied by her family so she hires a beautiful guy to be her fake boyfriend for the week,easy peasy,right?But she didn't remember that Christmas is a magic time and sometimes also the unthinkable suddenly becomes reality.<br /><br />I loved A Christmas Date,it was such an enjoyable,warm,funny and low dramatic read that put me right into a Christmassy mood.<br />I really liked how the plot developped and how all the characters were well portrayed.<br />I highly recommend to read this story and even if it is a standalone I suggest you to also read the previous books in the series because they are worth it. </p><br /><p> Copy kindly provided by the Publisher/Author. </p><br /></span>

<div id="review_2581268060" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2581268060" />
    <a title="Alison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27476718-alison"><img alt="Alison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451665348p2/27476718.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2581268060?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alison" href="/user/show/27476718-alison">Alison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2581268060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10612081717859062380">Yes it’s another Christmas book, there is always the danger that once you have read one ‘Festive’ book for the season that they will all become to sound, look, read the same. I mean how many different angles can they take? Add into that, the story line of dating or faking, it’s not a new notion either. <br/><br/>But do you know what … why I actually overlooked all those aspects? It’s because it’s Camilla Isley. And Camilla has a delightful way of telling a story and reeling the reader in with her cute but</span>
  <span id="freeText10612081717859062380" style="display:none">Yes it’s another Christmas book, there is always the danger that once you have read one ‘Festive’ book for the season that they will all become to sound, look, read the same. I mean how many different angles can they take? Add into that, the story line of dating or faking, it’s not a new notion either. <br /><br />But do you know what … why I actually overlooked all those aspects? It’s because it’s Camilla Isley. And Camilla has a delightful way of telling a story and reeling the reader in with her cute but effective funny, cosy stories.<br /><br />I have read books by her before so knew I was likely to feel as though I had met an old friend once I started A Christmas Date and I wasn’t far wrong. I think a lot of her success is having likeable characters that are totally believable and when you meet the hired ‘date’ Diego you will see what I mean, it always eases the reader in when there is a suitable hunk to drool over. <br /><br />Poor Nikki has been having a bad time and could quite happily hibernate for the whole Christmas holiday, who hasn’t felt like that at some point so that immediately drew me to her. I liked Nikki while she was a sassy gorgeous girl loved by all, she still wants a date to take home to show the family.<br /><br />A Christmas Date is a fun, quick book to read,it will soon have you finding out how Nikki copes with all the usual issues surrounding the time of year and families. Curl up with a cup of tea and prepare to enjoy and if necessary pretend this is your Christmas, because at least a book has the chance of a happy ending!<br /><br />Thanks to the author, publisher and Rachel from Random Resources. I read and reviewed voluntarily.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10612081717859062380" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2572832357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer192013615323454629">This review was first published at M's Bookshelf - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://mssbookshelf.blogspot.com'>http://mssbookshelf.blogspot.com</a><br/><br/>What an absolute must-read this holiday season! 'A Christmas Date' is the third installment in Camilla Isley's 'First Comes Love' series, but not having read the previous two myself, I can honestly say it can easily be read as a stand alone novel. Although, like me, I'm sure you'll be wanting to read those previous two the second you finish this one.<br/><br/>Starting the story off with a hired fake boyfriend, this could ha</span>
  <span id="freeText192013615323454629" style="display:none">This review was first published at M's Bookshelf - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://mssbookshelf.blogspot.com">http://mssbookshelf.blogspot.com</a><br /><br />What an absolute must-read this holiday season! 'A Christmas Date' is the third installment in Camilla Isley's 'First Comes Love' series, but not having read the previous two myself, I can honestly say it can easily be read as a stand alone novel. Although, like me, I'm sure you'll be wanting to read those previous two the second you finish this one.<br /><br />Starting the story off with a hired fake boyfriend, this could have gone very cheesy and predictable very soon. But Nikki and Diego took me by surprise. I ended up loving them, and their... 'adventure' much more than I would have thought. Christmas time and all the excitement and drama it brings with it, some disastrous cooking and a sexy romance, I absolutely loved every page.<br /><br />Highly addictive and entertaining, Camilla Isley will bring a smile to your face and will have you humming Christmas songs all day long, holiday season or not!</span>

          </span>

This book was sweet and hot like a hot chocolate with marshmallows...<br/><br/>There were family shenanigans, bickering, cute moments, a lovable protagonist, a dashing leading man, a great love story, the perfect best friend, and a full cast of adorable pets, all wrapped up in the Christmas sparkle...<br/><br/>I adored everything about this book! </span>

<div id="review_2615633064" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2615633064?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17629777-kelly-schnorrbusch?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17629777-kelly-schnorrbusch?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17629777-kelly-schnorrbusch?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17629777-kelly-schnorrbusch?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17629777-kelly-schnorrbusch?shelf=christmas">christmas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17629777-kelly-schnorrbusch?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2615633064" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16194316457540830294">This was such a fun little romance. I love the Rent-A-Date trope and if loving it is wrong, I don’t wanna be right! If those made for TV holiday movies are a little too much for you, try this book instead. It captures the spirit of the holiday season, but leaves out the ugly Christmas sweaters, lessons from a wise, old villager, and the shrill voices of former child actors. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1543964312ra/26690139.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Nikki is in love with her old friend Paul, who has been dating her younger sister Julia for 2 years when Julia announces th</span>
  <span id="freeText16194316457540830294" style="display:none">This was such a fun little romance. I love the Rent-A-Date trope and if loving it is wrong, I don’t wanna be right! If those made for TV holiday movies are a little too much for you, try this book instead. It captures the spirit of the holiday season, but leaves out the ugly Christmas sweaters, lessons from a wise, old villager, and the shrill voices of former child actors. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1543964312ra/26690139.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nikki is in love with her old friend Paul, who has been dating her younger sister Julia for 2 years when Julia announces their engagement! When their mother asks Nikki to give up her bedroom back home for the newly engaged couple during Christmas vacation, Nikki does what any sensible single woman would do under the circumstances – lie. She’ll be bringing a boyfriend home, too. So what if her boyfriend Diego is a paid actor, who just happens to be her sister’s ideal man? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543964416i/26690160._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nikki is a bit impulsive, but not recklessly so. She makes an intriguing main character that I think many modern, single women can relate to – hardworking, independent, and a strained family dynamic. Her best friend since childhood, Blair, is funny and supportive, but not blindly so. We all need a BFF to call us out on our shit sometimes and make sure we aren’t self-sabotaging ourselves.<br>Nikki’s sister Julia is hardest to like, but she is also the most like a caricature of all the things a suddenly- vegan Bridezilla can be. If that hits too close to home, just take a shot and keep reading. You know, like you do at your family gatherings. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1543964312ra/26690141.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This might be a bit predictable, but it really is fun and just the sort of book I needed right now – not too Christmasy, some kissing, a hot guy, some laughs, and a dog. After reading this I realized it is actually book 3 in a series, but it absolutely stands on it’s own. I found nothing lacking, but I do want to go back to the previous two books in the series. All opinions are my own, but I would like to thank Net Galley, the publisher, and author for providing a copy of the book.<br></span>

<div id="review_2578010767" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2578010767" />
    <a title="Anniek" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46780725-anniek"><img alt="Anniek" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451833768p2/46780725.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2578010767?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anniek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anniek" href="/user/show/46780725-anniek">Anniek</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2578010767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3124013562736526141">Nikki isn't a fan of the Christmas season. Her boss always closes the company during the Christmas holidays, thus leaving her no excuse to not be with her family. Ever since she met Paul in college Nikki secretly has a crush on him. Even when he was off limits because he was dating her sister Julia, her feelings for him didn't go away. When Julia tells Nikki that she and Paul are engaged and that he'll be spending the holidays with their family, Nikki has no idea how she is going to survive the </span>
  <span id="freeText3124013562736526141" style="display:none">Nikki isn't a fan of the Christmas season. Her boss always closes the company during the Christmas holidays, thus leaving her no excuse to not be with her family. Ever since she met Paul in college Nikki secretly has a crush on him. Even when he was off limits because he was dating her sister Julia, her feelings for him didn't go away. When Julia tells Nikki that she and Paul are engaged and that he'll be spending the holidays with their family, Nikki has no idea how she is going to survive the Christmas days. Can Nikki find a way to make the upcoming days more bearable?<br /><br />After talking with her best friend Blair, Nikki decides to hire a fake boyfriend who'll accompany her to her parents house. This way they won't see her as the pathetic single and she won't have to endure her mom's comments. Luckily Nikki works at an advertising agency so she has a whole database filled with good looking actors. To annoy her sister she searches for an actor who has all the characteristics her sister would look for in an ideal boyfriend. Diego is the perfect match. Diego agrees to be her fake boyfriend during the holidays but can they fool Nikki's family?<br /><br />Nikki feels like she always needs to compete with her beautiful sister. To her Julia, is perfect in every single way. When Julia started dating Paul, Nikki's heart shattered. She never thought that she'd find another man who'd make her feel the same way but spending time with Diego is heart warming. Nikki works hard, is a perfectionist and keeps most people at arms length. Even though she is a bit of a Grinch I had a connection with Nikki from the start. I was wishing for her to find the courage to open up her heart for love again.<br /><br />A Christmas Date is a feel good love story filled with humor and Christmas festivities. I absolutely love Christmas and I truly believe it's the most magical time of the year. Nikki's family loves Christmas as well and her mom went into full decorating mode. I could easily imagine what the house looked like and I wish I could visit Nikki's family as well. Unwrapping presents around the Christmas tree always fills my heart with joy and I couldn't wait to find out more about the blossoming love between Nikki and Diego. Camilla Isley never disappoints her readers with her lighthearted romantic novels and A Christmas Date is another fun and sweet story that I highly recommend. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3124013562736526141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2087103182" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2087103182" />
    <a title="Charanya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54727721-charanya"><img alt="Charanya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523903643p2/54727721.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2087103182?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Charanya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Charanya" href="/user/show/54727721-charanya">Charanya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54727721-charanya?shelf=4-almost-perfect-stars">4-almost-perfect-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2087103182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12844477690710389874"><b> 4.25 stars </b><br/><br/>I have read every single book by Camilla Isley, can't say that for any other author, except for maybe Rowling. Camilla has the ability to weave a heart melting romantic comedy even if you know there are going to be standard tropes. So much so that every new book comes through I inhale them at feverish speed. "A Christmas Date" was no exception, this romantic comedy trope is fairly tried and tested in movies and other books but still the author breathes fresh air into it. You know how</span>
  <span id="freeText12844477690710389874" style="display:none"><b> 4.25 stars </b><br /><br />I have read every single book by Camilla Isley, can't say that for any other author, except for maybe Rowling. Camilla has the ability to weave a heart melting romantic comedy even if you know there are going to be standard tropes. So much so that every new book comes through I inhale them at feverish speed. "A Christmas Date" was no exception, this romantic comedy trope is fairly tried and tested in movies and other books but still the author breathes fresh air into it. You know how the book is going to end, there are some cliches, some sibling drama and a really charming leading man but you still read on because the banter is lovely, the chemistry is swoon worthy. The author has the ability to inject the right amount of tension when she creates either the first kiss or the first meet. Here the meeting is supposed to be contractual, so that's less exciting but the lead up to their romance is fantastic. My only grouse is that this book needed to be longer and also <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ it's tough to buy her years of obsession with Paul snapping off just like that no matter how fantastic Diego is  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But these are minor complaints in an otherwise festive read. It was great to have Blair and Chevron back too<br /><br />The book earns marginally less than a 5 because nothing comes close to the epic romance of Blair and Richard in "I Have Never" and because the career takes a backstage here because there's no conflict there. Just romance and family drama which has a way of resolving itself towards the end leading to a happily ever after. <br /><br />As always, looking forward to future books from Camilla. The books are no longer just an auto-buy they demand immediate reading too!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12844477690710389874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2577133075" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2577133075" />
    <a title="booksofallkinds" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56398437-booksofallkinds"><img alt="booksofallkinds" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464775666p2/56398437.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2577133075?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="booksofallkinds" class="user" itemprop="url" name="booksofallkinds" href="/user/show/56398437-booksofallkinds">booksofallkinds</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2577133075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7212053506899944374">After a slightly hectic day, I decided to pick up A CHRISTMAS DATE by Camilla Isley and I am so glad I did because it really made me smile and relax. <br/><br/>​Nikki has a successful career that she works really hard at and close friends that she adores but with the Christmas holidays at home with her family looming, she is definitely not in the Christmas spirit. Nikki loves her family but it's hard having to listen about her perfect sister and her perfect fiancé - the guy who used to be her best friend </span>
  <span id="freeText7212053506899944374" style="display:none">After a slightly hectic day, I decided to pick up A CHRISTMAS DATE by Camilla Isley and I am so glad I did because it really made me smile and relax. <br /><br />​Nikki has a successful career that she works really hard at and close friends that she adores but with the Christmas holidays at home with her family looming, she is definitely not in the Christmas spirit. Nikki loves her family but it's hard having to listen about her perfect sister and her perfect fiancé - the guy who used to be her best friend and should have fallen in love with her. So during another phone call from her mother, Nikki makes up a boyfriend and soon finds herself hiring an actor for the holidays - a handsome, kind, considerate guy who could just be her perfect match if she could just let go of the past. <br /><br />With mishaps, sizzling chemistry, and home truths coming to light, A CHRISTMAS DATE by Camilla Isley has everything you need to make you feel all warm and fuzzy and put a smile on your face. Yes, the story did automatically remind me of the movie The Wedding Date, but it still brings fresh characters with their own issues, tension, and charisma, so don't let that put you off. The characters are really well-rounded, and I loved the close relationship that Nikki and Blair share. Diego is everything you want and more in this story and is sure to make your heart flutter. <br /><br />A CHRISTMAS DATE by Camilla Isley is fun, flirty, and filled with family messiness and I thoroughly enjoyed it from start to finish. Definitely a must for the Christmas season. <br /><br />*I voluntarily reviewed this book from the tour organiser</span>
  <a data-text-id="7212053506899944374" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText9766127582632065450" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this book.  It is the first I have read by Camilla Isley, but I really enjoyed her style of writing.  The story flowed flawlessly and I was interested to see how Nikki managed to cope with her overpowering parents and attention seeking sister, at the most stressful time of the year.<br />The story starts as Nikki is dreading Christmas and spending time with her family and her gloating sister, who is thrilled that Nikki’s one true love has proposed to her.  Her only friend Blair is also loved up with the man of her dreams, and being the only single person at Christmas is a truly terrifying thought for her.<br />So she puts her job to good use and comes up with a plan, that will not only silence her parents but will make her sister green with envy.  This is how she meets Diego, straight off the cover off a magazine.<br />Will she be able to pull off a great Christmas coup?  Or will her parents and sister see through her scam?<br />A lovely feel good Christmas read.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8zW4xw9l36c3spX55dCWZQxkJk6qHl5wBQHuvcs0JsTPDI31WYdz0KqcIpES1ZdtKy/X+FTSPsfnMmhTfR9weA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/AsVwzv0BulUEMjw1Vx94VnRI/9n2+kigiBJizFEtUXAMiDxbRaqnsk+f5giWXzpfprSSZkXiZVgE89lh2/j+Q==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1086683545354660091">Camilla is an engineer turned writer after she quit her job to follow her husband on an adventure abroad.<br/>She's a cat lover, coffee addict, and shoe hoarder. Besides writing, she loves reading--duh!--cooking, watching bad TV, and going to the movies--popcorn, please. She's a bit of a foodie, nothing too serious. A keen traveler, Camilla knows mosquitoes play a role in the ecosystem, and she doesn't</span>
